Current Affairs Commentary

After Reading "The 23rd Year Business Report of Jin Cheng Bank" 23

— Ping

Among Chinese banks that annually compile business reports detailing the economic situation at home and abroad, as well as the bank's operational performance, and distribute them to shareholders, besides the two in Shanghai, recently Jin Cheng Bank has followed suit. We know that the two banks in Shanghai both belong to the Jiang-Zhe banking group, and their investment and lending interests seem to be centered in Shanghai and focused on the Yangtze River basin. However, Jin Cheng is different. Its head office is located in Tianjin, and it is a pillar among the "Four Northern Banks" (referring to Jin Cheng Bank, Yieh Commercial Bank, China & South Sea Bank, and the Continental Bank). It subtly holds the reins of the financial world in North China. Therefore, the manifestations of its active business are slightly different. At a time when the situation in North China is severe, the publication of this business report by the bank is of profound significance.

What the Jin Cheng Bank's business report reveals to us is that Jin Cheng Bank is not just an ordinary commercial bank. From an analysis and observation of its lending operations, in addition to general industrial and commercial businesses, its direction seems to focus on assisting transportation and mining industries and mineral products. The total of these two lending items accounts for about one-fifth of the total. The high proportion of this component is probably unmatched by any other bank. The prosperity or decline of railways and mining industries is related to the lifeblood of the national industry and commerce. The bank's authorities, with their unique vision, are dedicated to assisting this sector, which is of no small benefit to the national economy. Now, the government authorities are gradually seeing the beginnings of old road repairs, and the construction of new lines is also being actively carried out, and mining merchants in various places are also making great efforts to reorganize in order to seek revitalization. At this time, we have high expectations for the bank authorities, who have always supported the road and mining industries, hoping that they will take the development of road and mining as their future mission in addition to ordinary banking business. If this is the case, the foundation of China's specialized banks can be expected to be established, and its effectiveness will far outweigh the wandering and indecisiveness of today's general commercial banks.

From a financial perspective, the fiercest competition with our banking and money industry comes from foreign banks. However, the existing capital of Chinese banks is still insufficient to compete with those backed by international capital. Therefore, if the Chinese banking sector wants to compete with foreign banks and navigate the international financial market, it must first increase its capital. For the sake of increasing capital, there are precedents in various countries for bank alliances and mergers. Money shops and small banks should be encouraged to unite or merge. Even large banks should also make this preparation as a leader. In this way, the entire front of our banking and money industry can be expected to be consolidated. The bank and the authorities of the "Four Northern Banks" had long seen that bank alliances are the way out for China's financial industry. The organization of the Four Banks Reserve Treasury Savings Association in the 12th year of the Republic, and the establishment of the Four Banks Joint Business Office last year, both pioneered the trend in China's financial sector. The capital increase and expansion of the Taiping Insurance Company (jointly established by the Four Banks and the Bank of Communications and China National Bank) is even more a manifestation of cooperation among the industry. However, in our view, the joint operation of several banks may still be insufficient to meet the future needs of China's financial industry. The most effective method seems to still need further unity.

The publication of Jin Cheng Bank's business report is still a first attempt. However, its broad perspective and detailed analysis can be called unprecedented. However, it seems to still focus on Shanghai in the domestic economic situation and fails to analyze and penetrate the changes in the economic status of North China, the rise and fall of Tianjin Port, and the rise and fall of industries. This is perhaps a slight disappointment for those seeking economic research data on North China.

Local Officials in Songpan Prefecture of Sichuan Province Request That the Establishment of Counties Across Borders in Qinghai Province Be Stopped 24

(Chongqing) Wan Qing, a local official of Luo Kangsa in Songpan Prefecture, and others wired the provincial government, stating that Qinghai Province recently established Tongde County at Tula Jia Temple, specifically to control the Golok tribes, and repeatedly sent personnel to collect tea and water fees, and ordered them to surrender. The Former Ministry of Communications in Beijing Owes the Electrical Company for Materials 37

(Nanjing) The former Ministry of Communications in Beijing owed the China Electrical Company for materials, totaling US$1,513,378 as of the end of last year. If the company has no profit or loss, the interest will be waived. If the dividends exceed 3% of the share amount, the excess will be used as repayment. When the principal reaches US$900,000, the account will be cleared. (16th Special Telegram)

French Chamber of Deputies Passes Extension of Military Service Bill, Extending from One Year to Two Years, Strengthening Military Strength, Germany Also Announces Immediate Implementation of Conscription 58

(Paris) When the government of Dunsu sleeves made an important statement this morning in Congress when passing the bill to extend the term of military service, it was rumored that Britain and the Soviet Union had requested France to increase the number of active servicemen. Congress passed the bill to increase the term of military service from one year to two years by 389 votes to 190 votes. Military experts declared that the bill could in fact double the number of active servicemen in France. According to the number of soldiers in France's army, it is second only to the Soviet Union. After passing the bill, Congress passed the government's confidence vote by 354 votes to 210 votes. Observers believe that Helleu's remarks are noteworthy. Helleu declared to Congress, "If you know what we know, then no one in Congress will oppose the government." Some members of Congress believe that Helleu's words imply that Britain and the Soviet Union have requested France to increase its military strength. When Premier Flandin debated the bill, he cited Germany's rearmament, saying, "Now we can prove with numbers that the expansion of Germany's military strength is enough to put France's army in danger. Since Germany withdrew from the League of Nations, the relationship between France and Germany has changed. Since then, it has violated the Treaty of Versailles and carried out the restoration of military equipment." According to the military service bill passed today, the term of service for those who enlist in mid-April will be increased to 18 months, and the term of service for subsequent grades will be two years. (15th National Telegram)

(Paris) The French government issued a declaration today, stating that Germany had violated the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles restricting its armaments and intended to establish an air force. The declaration was issued in both the Senate and the House of Representatives, stating that when Germany unilaterally increased its combat strength, France's combat strength could not be allowed to fall for a moment. The French government cannot tolerate Germany's actions more than the British government. The term of military service for new recruits called up in mid-April 1935 has been increased from one year to 18 months. Those called up in mid-October 1935 and those called up in the next four years will be increased to two years. The government has submitted a bill to the House of Representatives today, stipulating that the age of military service will be gradually reduced from 21 to 20 and that mercenaries will be recruited. The bill clearly states that this plan is not intended to increase the regular quota of 230,000 soldiers, but to make up for the decrease in the birth rate in the years of the war. If this is not done, France's army will be reduced to 118,000 by 1940. The conclusion of the government's declaration calls on Congress to inspire patriotism, agree with the government's measures, and said that the military equipment maintained by France is only necessary to protect peace and security and to prevent aggressors from achieving their desires. (15th Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) The German government has decided on Germany's general military equipment and will immediately implement a compulsory military service system. Today, German leader Hitler issued a proclamation on this matter, and Minister of Propaganda Goebbels read this document to foreign news interviewers. What is now known is that Germany's peacetime standing army will be 12 legions and 36 divisions. (16th Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) Today, after learning that the French parliament passed a bill to extend military service, newspapers here have used headlines such as "France dealt a fatal blow to disarmament," "France is the gravedigger of disarmament," and "Disarmament is dead" to write about it on the front page. The newspapers also wrote critical remarks, unanimously expressing disappointment with France's policy of expanding its military strength. (16th National Telegram)

Debates in the French Chamber of Deputies on the Military Service Bill: The Socialist Party Appeals for Peace and Opposes a Napoleonic-Style Army 59

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies today discussed the bill to extend the term of military service until late into the night. After Prime Minister Flandin explained the reasons for the government's proposal, Socialist Deputy Blum, representing the orthodox Socialist Party, spoke out against extending the term of military service, advocating "making the most sublime appeal for peace to the world." He stated that the government's proposed two-year military service bill was intended to improve the quality of the army and that the situation was similar to that of 1913-1914. He claimed that the government was preparing a large-scale Napoleonic-style offensive plan. Following this, Foppé, Chairman of the Chamber of Deputies' Army Committee, analyzed the current state of the German army and its military supplies. Foppé stated, "Regarding the state of French military preparations, there is no reason for Germany to rearm. Germany should bear sole responsibility for the expansion of armaments. In the past year, Germany has increased its defense forces from 200,000 to 600,000 men, and its reserve forces from 100,000 to 400,000 men. The military industry is intensifying its work, and all civilian aviation has been converted to military aviation. This warmongering spirit of Germany inevitably makes all of Europe, and even Russia, uneasy. Now, the French government cannot propose a clear and frank military bill, leaving the size of the French army uncertain and making mobilization difficult. This is regrettable." Foppé also stated that the general advocacy of abolishing the army is despicable. One should know that the Soviet Red Army has also increased from 600,000 to 940,000 men. In conclusion, he stated, "I am deeply aware of our people's belief in peace and their desire for security, but the cabinet's declaration is far from sufficient." During the Chamber of Deputies' recess, the Radical Party held a caucus. After a speech by Minister Without Portfolio Herriot, the entire caucus voted to support the government's proposal, with 30 deputies abstaining. Subsequently, the Chamber of Deputies continued the debate, and it is expected that a vote on the bill will not be taken until late into the night. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Paris) The bill to extend the term of military service has been passed in the Chamber of Deputies. The discussion and voting situation is as follows: A Communist deputy rose to speak against it after Foppé, Chairman of the Army Committee, saying that the two-year military service system is a threat of a new war. Former Minister of Finance Reynaud of the Republican Center Party stated that most countries, such as Britain, Switzerland, and Czechoslovakia, have reluctantly increased military spending due to Hitler's Germany. In France, it is necessary to focus on the substance of the army and form elite troops composed of specialized personnel in order to resist attacks. Minister Without Portfolio Herriot, leader of the Radical Socialist Party, enthusiastically supported the bill to extend the term of military service, saying, "The news is very serious. What you know may not be as detailed as what I know. Otherwise, your applause and support will be the first to come." Former Prime Minister Daladier of the same party believed that reorganizing the army was better than extending the term of military service. Independent Deputy Pouis said that he opposed gradually extending military service to two years and advocated extending it directly. When the debate concluded, various parties proposed a total of three motions: (1) proposed by the Socialist Party, stating, "The Chamber of Deputies refuses to increase the military burden before seeking public opinion." The government raised a vote of confidence on this motion, and the Chamber of Deputies rejected it by a vote of 309 to 109. (2) Proposed by Foppé, Chairman of the Army Committee, expressing confidence in the government but demanding that the government propose a bill to reorganize the army, with the situation of German rearmament as the goal. The government opposed this motion and also raised a vote of confidence, which the Chamber of Deputies rejected by a vote of 530 to 44. Socialist deputies also voted against this motion. (3) Proposed by former Minister of Aviation Laurent-Eynac, stating, "The Chamber of Deputies trusts the government and expresses its approval of the government's declaration." The government accepted this motion and raised a vote of confidence. As a result, the Chamber of Deputies finally passed it by a vote of 350 to 196. Among the deputies of the Radical Socialist Party, only 32 voted against it, and the rest expressed their support. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Simon's Speech: The Mission to Tour Europe Is of Great Importance; The Success or Failure of Disarmament Hinges on This Trip 61

Foreign Secretary Sir John Simon delivered a speech in Swansea today, vigorously defending Britain's increase in defense capabilities. He also said that if he and Lord Privy Seal Eden can achieve success during their upcoming tour of Europe, a disarmament convention may be concluded, and the League of Nations and the collective peace system may be consolidated as a result. Simon also cited the Manchurian problem, clarifying the difficulty of resolving international disputes by invoking the principles of the League of Nations, stating that the League of Nations' handling of the Manchurian incident has caused Japan to withdraw from the League of Nations, but some people are still demanding more severe measures. Simon further stated that the recent actions of Japan, Germany, Russia, and the United States have not only failed to disarm but have expanded armaments. (National News Agency dispatch, 16th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon recently delivered a speech in Swansea, Wales, outlining the visit to Berlin, stating, "If this visit to Germany can achieve something, it will not only help ease the European situation but also make it possible for the disarmament agreement we have been longing for to be established. The British government also attaches great importance to Lord Privy Seal Eden's visit to Russia and Poland. Our visits to these three countries are of great significance. We sincerely hope to obtain the sincere cooperation of the governments of these three countries to promote international understanding, as international understanding is what we are most concerned about. Moreover, peace is not a partial issue but the main goal of British foreign policy, and it is also the common expectation of all the British people. Some people believe that Britain does not have the firm intention to support the League of Nations, and there is no greater fallacy than this, because the British government is committed to building a collective system to maintain peace." (London) The Havas Agency's correspondent in London has learned that British diplomatic circles believe that before Britain and Germany discuss the issue of German rearmament in Berlin, the German government and British cabinet members must first reach a principled agreement on the East European Mutual Assistance Pact. How to restore friendly relations between Germany and the Soviet Union will be the first goal of the Anglo-German talks in Berlin. After this issue is resolved, the second issue, the conclusion of a Danube River Pact to guarantee Austria's independence, will be discussed. As a third step, British cabinet members will ask Germany to sign an arms limitation treaty. Only after the above security issues are resolved can the issue of German rearmament continue to be discussed. However, no final conclusion can be reached on the issue of German rearmament during the period when British cabinet members visit Berlin. After Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden return to their country, they will first report to the British cabinet on the results achieved on security issues and rearmament issues, and then consult with the French and Italian governments before the British government can make a final decision. Assassination Attempt on the King of Hejaz: Yemeni Attacks During Prayers; Foiled by Guards 65

(London) According to a statement issued by the Hejaz Embassy in London, King Ibn Saud of Hejaz and Nejd and his eldest son, Emir Saud, narrowly escaped assassination during morning prayers today. As the King was circling the Kaaba four times, several people suddenly rushed towards the King with sharp blades. Just before the King reached the Black Stone, the leader of the assassins lunged at him. Seeing this, the Crown Prince stepped forward to block him, and the assassin retreated slightly. Just as he was about to move forward again, a guard shot and killed him. At that time, the other assassins attacked the Crown Prince, but before they could strike, they were all knocked down by the guards. The King and the Crown Prince calmly completed the seven rounds of circling the Kaaba. After the ceremony, they happily received the delegation that came to offer congratulations, as is customary after completing the pilgrimage to the holy site. The assassins were all Zaydis from Yemen. It is said that Ibn Saud fought with Yemen last year, so the purpose of this assassination must have been revenge. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Murphy also listed the Philippines' urgent needs as follows: (1) $1 million for public works, flood control projects, sanitation, and road construction; (2) $100,000 to eradicate locusts in the Philippines; (3) An investigation of food to adjust production restriction plans, with expenses of $25,000; (4) Reclamation of wasteland, with expenses of $1 million; (4) Purchase of sugar. Belgium Maintains the Gold Standard: Meetings with France Today; European Countries Compete to Purchase Sterling 69

(London) The anxiety caused by Belgium's maintenance of the gold standard has led European countries to compete to purchase sterling today, so the price of sterling in terms of dollars and other gold coins has suddenly rebounded. The dollar fell from $4.75625 to $4.7975, the French franc fell from 72.09 to 72.78, and the Belgian franc fell from 20.37 to 20.59. The market price fluctuated greatly throughout the day due to public unrest. Belgian franc transactions have recently been quite difficult, as today's one-month term discount rate is nominally 70 centimes, while the three-month term discount rate is 120 centimes. As a result of the rebound in sterling, the price of gold fell by one shilling and seven and a half pence per net ounce to 146 shillings and a half pence, and then to 145 shillings. However, due to the unstable exchange rate trend, many buyers are hesitant. The stock exchange is currently discussing what impact gold will have if the "gold bloc" collapses. Insiders say that when the United States is preparing to purchase at a price of $35 per ounce and the New York-London exchange rate is below $5, the price of gold must be above 140 shillings. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Norwegian Cabinet Resigns: Conflict of Opinion on Unemployment Relief Bill; First Labor Government to Be Formed 70

Oslo: The Norwegian Liberal Party government, formed by Mowinckel on March 1, 1933, has been stable, but today the Labor Party in the parliament demanded increased funding to alleviate unemployment. The government opposed it, saying that if so, the tax rate would inevitably increase. When the vote was taken, the Labor Party's proposal was passed by 95 votes to 55, so the government resigned immediately. The Labor Party is currently forming a new government, with Speaker of Parliament Nygaardsvold as Prime Minister. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Oslo: Liberal Prime Minister Mowinckel announced that the current government will resign today, predicting that Norway will have its first Labor cabinet. According to official sources, King Haakon VII will appoint Labor leader Nygaardsvold to form a new government. Prime Minister Mowinckel refused the request of the leaders of the Labor and Farmers' Parties to increase emergency funds by 10 million kroner, and the parliament immediately passed a vote of no confidence in the government. The Mowinckel cabinet then resigned. Observers say that the requested funds would have to be met by issuing bonds or increasing taxes. Parliament passed the vote of no confidence by 94 votes to 65. It is said that Mowinckel's resignation this time is similar to the situation when he took office as Prime Minister for the third time. Observers say that Norway's exports in 1934 accounted for the highest amount since the war, so some cabinet members did not believe that it was necessary to increase 10 million kroner. Norway's officially announced unemployment rate is about 35,000, slightly higher than last year, but the government believes that since business has the prospect of prosperity, it should be able to absorb these unemployed people in a short period of time. It is now heard that Nygaardsvold will be ordered to form a new cabinet. Nygaardsvold is the speaker of the upper house and has been involved in the labor movement for a long time. The Norwegian Labor Party does not belong to the Second or Third International and is more radical than other Labor parties in Europe, and it also occupies more seats in parliament than other political parties, so it is not yet certain whether Nygaardsvold will ask other political parties to participate in the formation of the cabinet. (National News Agency dispatch, 15th)

Japanese House of Representatives: Commends Yukio Ozaki for Over Thirty Years of Struggle for Constitutional Government 71

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives met at 1:00 p.m. today to hold a commendation ceremony for Representative Yukio Ozaki. Ozaki has been continuously elected as a representative for more than thirty years since the Japanese government opened the first Diet. To this day, his contribution to constitutional government has been great. Vice-Speaker Uehara was the first to take the podium, explaining Ozaki's active involvement in the political world and his various contributions. Then, he proposed to commend Ozaki, requesting everyone's consent. With unanimous approval, the proposal was passed. After Speaker Hamada read the commendation, Ozaki took the stage to give a speech. His speech was as follows: "I am overwhelmed with gratitude for the commendation from you today. However, I regret that I cannot share this happy event with Mr. Inukai Tsuyoshi, who has worked together for politics since the first Imperial Diet." (Applause from the whole house) "I am not the only one who has struggled for constitutional government, but it is regrettable that those who are still alive receive this honor, while the dead have not seen this move. If the two major political parties today are healthy and developed and see the commendation, there is no greater joy than this. However, I am saddened by the current state of decline of political parties, and it is a great pain to see today's event. The majority of the responsibility for the decline of constitutional government should be borne by us, and I am extremely ashamed to be commended by you today." Ozaki then spoke in detail about the decline of political parties, and the hall was silent. Ozaki continued, "I have served as a minister twice and have been awarded the rank of Senior Third Rank and the First Order of Merit. However, many have struggled for constitutional government for forty-three years without receiving this grace, and the world does not find it strange. This is evidence of a lack of understanding of constitutional politics and a sign of respecting officials and despising the people." Ozaki's words of gratitude for the commendation turned into a fierce denunciation of the current government. Ozaki then turned his criticism to the political parties, saying that the reason for the corruption of political parties lies in the fact that they cannot gain power without money or power. This is something you are already familiar with. Ozaki then gave various warnings and bitter words to each political party before descending from the podium, and the whole hall applauded thunderously. (United Press dispatch, 16th)

Sharp Increase in British Silver Exports 74

(London) In the one-week period ending on Wednesday of this week, the quantity of British silver exports sharply increased. Its value increased by £836,000 compared to last week, totaling £1,110,000. The United States purchased the most, taking away £860,000. India took £355,000. China took £251,000. The Netherlands also purchased £22,000. British silver imports this week totaled £439,000, an increase of £213,000 compared to last week, almost doubling. Among them, those from the Far East were the most. India came with £109,000. Japan came with £87,000. Russia came with £93,000. The Netherlands came with £40,000. Czechoslovakia came with £36,000. France came with £25,000. Compared to this week's silver imports and exports, the net export value was £1,072,000, an increase of £462,000 compared to last week. (Reuters, March 15)

Northwest Inspection Journal 99

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya

A Glimpse of the Second Hami Incident

The indigenous ethnic groups of Xinjiang, since the Han Dynasty, have been nurtured by the culture of the Central Plains for over two thousand years. The emotions of the various ethnic groups, both old and new, residing together, have generally entered a stage of harmony. Although occasional ripples may arise, even evolving into a prairie fire situation, examining the driving force, it mostly does not originate from the lower masses of various ethnic groups but rather stems from a single thought of a few chieftains and leaders. If this thought is evil, bloodshed can occur for a thousand miles, as mentioned in the previous article regarding the widespread turmoil in Xinjiang. If this thought is good, it can easily transform conflict into friendship, as seen in the rise and fall of the Second Hami Incident described in this article.

The Second Hami Incident, tracing its beginning and end, resembles a sudden attack of stormy waves, arriving unexpectedly and then retreating swiftly. The main protagonist is Dr. Yao Lebos, the central figure of the previous turmoil. In February of the 23rd year [of the Republic of China, 1934], Ma Zhongying besieged Dihua but failed and retreated south. Yao, originally a staunch opponent of the new government, upon hearing the news in Turpan, quickly led his remaining troops to Hami and surrendered to the provincial government. He was appointed as the acting county magistrate and commander of the city defense. By August, the provincial government concluded its military affairs in southern Xinjiang and turned its attention to Hami as an important eastern route. Liu Yingpo was appointed as the administrative director, and a certain Xu was appointed as the garrison commander. Liu arrived in Hami first to take office, while Xu seemed to have reservations, arriving a month later with over four hundred elite soldiers, reaching Sanbao, three stations away from Hami.

Yao had an old relationship with Ma Zhongying. Although the provincial government entrusted him with an important battle, his heart was ultimately filled with unease. Now, upon learning of Xu's military affairs, he was even more frightened. Earlier, Nie Zier, the Little Prince of Hami, had a long-standing feud with Yao since childhood. After the death of the Sand King, Nie Zier inherited the position, and his relationship with Yao became even more strained. Although Yao still held the position of Chán [Muslim] tribe chief (bek) and continued as the battalion commander of the military camp, he did not go to the Prince's residence to work. This time, upon returning to Hami from Turpan, he disarmed Nie Zier's guards. Nie Zier was deeply resentful and secretly sent a confidant to Dihua, seeking help from Governor Sheng Shicai. Sheng specifically permitted Nie Zier to formally inherit the position and urged Xu to lead his troops to capture Hami as soon as possible. The confidant sent by Nie served as a guide for the army. Unexpectedly, he suddenly fled to Hami midway and revealed everything to Yao, saying that Xu's troops were actually coming to Hami to confiscate Yao's weapons to investigate his past crimes. He could not bear to see his fellow tribesmen being harmed, so he changed his mind and rushed to report the news. (Brothers quarreling at home defend against external aggression. Most ethnic groups who believe in Islam particularly possess this spirit.) Upon hearing this, Yao was filled with both gratitude and fear. He immediately appointed him as a regimental commander and secretly ordered all tribal families to hide in the mountains, with the able-bodied men supplementing the Chán army, setting up layers of defense on the western front. Nie Zier had just received a telegram from the province and posted a large red announcement of his inheritance in the Hui [Muslim] city when he was summoned by Yao to the new city and ordered to quickly produce one thousand taels of gold to prepare for Xu's troops' provisions. Nie was at a loss and was imprisoned for many days. Yao, having made up his mind to resist Xu, feared that preparations would be insufficient, so he pretended to discuss the matter of barracks and provisions with Administrative Director Liu Yinglin, requesting him to convey to Xu's troops to postpone their advance to Hami, allowing him to first communicate with the Chán people to facilitate a united welcome. In reality, the so-called communication was secretly dispatching chieftains to spread various anti-Xu propaganda to the Chán people. The Chán people, simple-minded, believed it to be true. The Kazakhs also echoed, declaring, "If Xu's army actually advances to Toubao (one station away from Hami city), we will first start by executing four Han Chinese leaders to resist the war. If they attack Toubao and advance to the garden city, and we cannot resist, we will decide to cleanse the city and retreat to the mountains." From then on, the whole city was in an uproar, as if a great disaster was imminent. Officials and gentry feared being the ones executed and felt a sense of impending doom. Subsequently, officials and gentry jointly telegraphed the provincial government repeatedly, requesting them to stop Xu's army from coming to Hami, with earnest wording, and the unspoken implication that Yao's troops could be held responsible. A certain chairman of the chamber of commerce also personally went to the military camp, requesting Xu not to advance hastily, but with Yao's welcoming representatives by his side, he ultimately did not dare to speak the truth directly. As Xu's army advanced to Erbao, the atmosphere suddenly became tense. Fortunately, the provincial government's order to stop arrived in time, and a delegation from the Han-Hui joint Hami team, led by a certain foreign advisor, came to Hami in two cars. Yao treated them with great courtesy and hosted a grand banquet. After the advisor was full and drunk, he ordered Yao to hand over the weapons. Yao obediently listened and casually pointed to several Chán soldiers, saying, "So-and-so is a brigade commander, so-and-so is a regimental commander. From now on, all military power will be lifted, and it would be great to focus on county affairs." The advisor, unaware of the reality, rejoiced that a great achievement had been accomplished with ease. Yao then handed over the county seal, resigning from the position of county magistrate. The representatives felt even more relieved and urged Yao to gather his troops for inspection. Yao initially refused, saying he had no authority. Then, Chán and Kazakh militiamen swarmed in and suddenly imprisoned the representatives, confiscating their vehicles and equipment. Only then did the advisor and others realize they had been tricked and were shocked. They agreed to immediately telegraph the governor's office, guaranteeing Yao's promotion to Hami District Garrison Commander in order to escape danger. Yao casually agreed. Later, the provincial telegram arrived, "Approved as requested." Yao then released them and returned them to Dihua, even holding a farewell conference before their departure, requesting them to leave one car behind and instructing them to convey to the governor's office, "Please do not be hostile in the future, and quickly withdraw Xu's army. The situation here is calm and there is no need to increase troops. Now that I have been appointed as the Hami District Garrison Commander, I will work even harder to maintain law and order." Although the advisor and others knew that this trip had failed, they had no choice but to agree and leave. Shortly after, King Nie Zier of Hami paid 260 taels of gold and was able to regain his freedom. Xu's army, which had advanced to Erbao, also retreated to Turpan. This scene of a dangerous situation with stormy waves was thus calmed.

Yao's father was from Hunan, and his mother was a Chán woman from southern Xinjiang (Southern Xinjiang Chán women occasionally intermarried with Han Chinese. Hami religious rules are very strict, Chán tribes are only allowed to marry Han women, not Han men.) He is nearly fifty years old and has taken his fourth wife. His eldest son, Daochang, also has four wives, one of whom is a Han woman. Chán people commonly have multiple wives, and according to religious rules, they are treated equally and do not have the status of concubines. The Steel Department consultant Sven Hedin and his party, on their way east, passed through Hami, and various agencies held banquets to bid them farewell. Yao especially treated them with courtesy, enjoying endless conversations. Someone jokingly said, "Hedin is a doctor, and Yao is also called a doctor. They met late in life, no wonder they are so attached to each other." The next morning, Hedin hurriedly left Hami, and Yao did not have time to see him off, jokingly telling the reporter, "This old man is traveling in a hurry, probably fearing that I would detain his car." Later, Hedin returned to Gansu territory and re-entered Xinjiang via Dunhuang, indeed lingering at the site of the ancient Loulan Kingdom for many days before returning east, which shows Yao's personality.

Jiangnan Defense Army Smashes the Main Force of Jiangxi Bandits 100

Annihilating Several Hundred Elements of the False Central Government; Key Figure Ruan Xiaoxian Also Shot Dead

Guangzhou Communication: The remnant bandits in Jiangnan, led by Ye Jianying, Chen Yi, Xiang Ying, and others, numbering about 40,000 to 50,000, have been stirring up trouble separately in recent days. On one hand, they are using scattered bandits to harass Jiangnan; on the other hand, they are sending bandits to attempt to cross the Hunan border to connect with Guizhou bandits. Therefore, in recent days, Jiangxi bandits have been invading southward through multiple routes. On the 4th of this month, about 2,000 members of the false 24th Division attacked Anyuan City from Huichang. Bandit traces were discovered in the Banshi and Chongshi areas. The [Unit/Division name unreadable due to blurring in source] regiment of the [Unit/Division name unreadable due to blurring in source] Division stationed in Xinfeng was dispatched to intercept them. They engaged in a major battle with the bandits on the 6th, and the bandits were unsuccessful. At the same time, a portion of the Communist bandits, led by Xiang Ying, Chen Yi, and Ye Jianying, also committed crimes near Ganxian through various routes. Our [Unit/Division name unreadable due to blurring in source] Division has been in intense battle with the bandits in the Jinsha, Xiazhu Keng, Shiliao, and Luokeng areas for three days and three nights. From the 4th to the 6th, they have already defeated the main force of the bandits. We have just received a telegram from Yu Hanmou on the 8th, stating that according to the face-to-face report from Division Commander Mo, the [Unit/Division name unreadable due to blurring in source] regiment annihilated the important central organs of the bandits on the 5th and 6th in Tangcun, on the border with Lingdu, killing over 300 bandits and capturing over 700, including important bandit criminals such as pseudo-Central Committee member Liu Bojian, Ruan Xiaoxian, and the chief of staff's secretary (according to reports, the key Communist bandit Ruan Xiaoxian was a member of the Communist bandit's pseudo-Central Committee, concurrently serving as a member of the pseudo-Jiangxi Provincial Committee, and key positions such as the pseudo-Central Secretary, and was shot dead in Shangshui Keng; this unit of bandits was the pseudo-General Supply Department, and the Jiangnan regiment, as well as the pseudo-24th Division), etc. According to the report from [Unit] Commander [Unreadable], our regiment encountered the Communist bandits' pseudo-Jiangnan Regiment 1, 2, and 3 at Jinsha, Shiliao, Yachikeng, and other places on the 5th and 6th, engaging in fierce battles all day, killing on the spot the pseudo-special envoy commander Luo Kehai, the pseudo-detachment leader, and over 200 others, capturing the pseudo-Jiangnan Military Region political director Liu Bojian, secretary Liao Gekun, chief of staff Ye Rulong, transportation section chief Lian Desheng, trade bureau director Wang Zhikai, and over 700 others, seizing 7 light machine guns and 450 rifles. According to the prisoners, the bandits attempted to develop guerrilla warfare to protect the Jiangnan bandit area. The bandits killed this time were the backbone of the pseudo-Jiangnan bandits. Our troops are currently searching the deep mountains around Tangcun, Shangshui Keng, and Luokeng. Yesterday, another telegram stated that several hundred bandits were near Changluo Ao on the 7th, and a team is currently being dispatched to suppress them. According to the captured bandits, this unit is the Yuxi Independent Battalion, coming from Lefeng, intending to secretly cross the west. Our First Regiment's two battalions have returned to Changluo and have been defeating the pseudo-Independent Third Regiment in the Diya Meiziyuan Tangtou Ao area for days, killing dozens including the pseudo-battalion commander and political commissar, and capturing dozens including the battalion and company commanders and political commissars. Haimen: Girl Buried in Inferno 103

The home of Zhu Ronggou, a villager in Nanli Xu, Central Street, Sanchang City, caught fire due to a child carelessly playing with matches at 10 AM yesterday. Suddenly, thick smoke filled the air, and flames soared. Zhu urgently called for neighbors to help put out the fire, but the wind was strong, and the fire spread rapidly, making it difficult to contain. In an instant, eight thatched houses and furniture were completely burned, and a five-year-old girl failed to escape and was buried in the inferno. The body was charred and horrifying to witness. Jiading: Meeting to Cover County Magistrate Wu's Deficit 104

When former County Magistrate Wu Bogeng left office, he owed the provincial government over 10,000 yuan. Later, considering that it was during the Communist bandit disturbances and the situation was special, the Department of Finance approved the write-off of over 3,900 yuan in administrative expenses overruns and over 4,800 yuan in special expenses related to bandit suppression, leaving a remaining deficit of over 3,319 yuan. The province ordered a strict pursuit. The county's public property department, etc., considered that former County Magistrate Wu had contributed greatly to bandit suppression, and the deficit owed to the province was due to public service, and requested the Department of Finance to waive the pursuit. The Department of Finance, based on the report, instructed the county government to convene a meeting of local agencies and groups on the 15th to discuss mitigation methods. It was resolved that since former County Magistrate Wu was unable to raise funds and the local government was unable to make up for the deficiency, but the deficit was incurred due to public service and was in response to special circumstances, the province should waive the pursuit.

Wuxi: Intense Battle Between Police and Bandits in Baitang Embankment 105

The river surface in the Baitang Embankment area of the county is wide and has always been a place where bandits emerge. Passing ships are often robbed. Around 9 PM the night before (the 15th), a civilian ship was passing through Baitang Embankment when it suddenly encountered three bandit ships with thirty to forty bandits, each armed with guns and weapons, trying to rob silver, foreign currency, and clothes. Upon seeing the situation, the crew frantically shouted for help. The No. 5 and No. 7 patrol boats of the Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team, stationed at Doumen Bridge, heard the news and immediately went to pursue them. Unexpectedly, the bandits opened fire to resist. Officer Ye Tingzhang of the No. 7 patrol boat led the police to return fire. The sound of gunfire was rapid and dense, like a string of pearls, lasting for four or five minutes. Officer Ye ran out of ammunition, so he ran to Qinxiang Town and notified the 34th detachment of the Shitouwan Chamber of Commerce by telephone, which then reported to the 15th detachment of Kaizhou and the security teams at Beiqifang Yanqiao, requesting each to send a team to assist. Seeing a large number of merchant groups arriving, the bandits were outnumbered and fled in all directions. In addition to dispatching all the staff of the Supervision Division and the detectives of the Detective Team, the Public Security Bureau also ordered the car patrol team to go to catch them. Yan Heling, the captain of the 9th detachment of the 2nd District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Public Security Bureau stationed in Wuxi, also sent Officer Xiang Wengui, leading more than ten team members, to rush to the Gaoqiao area to pursue them. Because it was night, there was no effective protection.

Shanghai Xinhua Foreign Company recently received a tip-off that the Xincheng Printing Factory on Jiaoji Road in this county was counterfeiting the trademark of Youteermi Bai Zhuo Wan, a drug sold by the company. Because the case was related to counterfeiting trademarks, the case was immediately submitted to the General Bureau, and yesterday, they were transferred to the local branch court for interrogation.

Changshu: Sanfeng Buddhist Hall Destroyed 107

Outside the North Gate of this county, there is a famous ancient temple called Qingliang Chan Temple (also known as Sanfeng Temple), a very popular incense burning site. It is currently presided over by Abbot Yixi, a monk who graduated from a certain Buddhist school in Japan. The temple was built in the Tang Dynasty and contains many ancient artifacts, books, and paintings. On the 12th of this month, Jiang Canran, the current manager of the local telephone company, Shen Zhuqing, the owner of the Kaitai Rice Mill, and Zhang Shenzhi, an engineer from Beijing, and others came. Because they were drinking too much, they complained that the monks were not hospitable enough, so they started arguing and actually destroyed the Buddhist hall (that is, the abbot's room). In addition to the table lamps and sundries on the table, three exquisite sandalwood wooden Buddha statues were broken, and the dharma seat was also overturned. Among them, there was also the most precious dragon head crutch (dharma staff), which was said to have been passed down from the Han Dynasty, and has been more than 500 years old. It was considered a rare treasure, and it was also broken. At that time, Jiang and Shen were reported to the police station and arrested. Now, the temple officials have hired lawyer Yu Chengmei to draft a complaint and sue in court.

Changzhou: Yunhe Lin Nan Heng Lin Section Begins Construction 108

Since the preparation for the dredging of the Lin Nan Heng Lin section of the Wuxi Yunhe Canal, the river water has been drained, and construction can begin. Yesterday, the town leaders Zhang Jun and Cai Tingyan convened a joint meeting of the township chiefs and local gentry merchants. At that time, it was decided: (1) Each township should recruit 20 laborers; (2) The laborers recruited should be locals in principle. If foreign laborers are involved, their safety must be the responsibility of the township chief; (3) Zhang Jun was appointed as the team leader, and Cai Tingyan, Feng Xiuji, Zhu Kongyang, and Yan Hanming were appointed as the group leaders; (4) Construction will begin simultaneously and uniformly on the 16th.

Jiashan: Battle Between Security Team and Lake Bandits 112

Wang Peishen, a wealthy kiln owner in the Podiexiegang area of the town of Xiadianmiao, had been coveted by lake bandits for a long time. His two brothers had been separated for a long time, so the bandits set their sights on Wang. Late at night a few days ago, two black awning boats carrying over 20 lake bandits speaking different dialects arrived in the harbor, broke down the front door, searched for Wang Peishen but failed to find him, and kidnapped Wang Peishen's wife, Li, and her young child, using hemp ropes to tie them up. At the same time, they robbed the rooms of Wang's two brothers, taking away all the valuable clothing. Wang Peishen's self-defense pistol was also taken by the bandits. The Xiadianmiao town security team, known for its bravery, heard the alarm and opened fire. The two sides began to fight fiercely for about an hour. The security team fired over 200 rounds. The bandits were overwhelmed and tried to escape. The 7th squadron of the water police happened to be chasing from Xitang in a shallow-water gunboat. The county government also sent a police brigade and basic team on the Xinming ship to encircle and suppress them via Ganyao. The bandits abandoned their loot and fled.

Xiaoshan: Unseasonable Weather Leads to Scarlet Fever Epidemic 114

The temperature in Xunshan has suddenly increased in recent days, with the Fahrenheit thermometer consistently reaching over 80 degrees at noon. Due to the unseasonable weather, smallpox and diphtheria are prevalent among the general population, with scarlet fever among the adults and smallpox among the children. Since the 12th, a total of over 20 people have died inside and outside the city. Yesterday, Wang Fengzhi's young son in the west gate, a young girl surnamed Mao outside the east gate, and Zhao Chunfang in the west gate died of diphtheria. Western and Chinese doctors are extremely busy recently.

The Yangjiadu Wharf and Warehouses of the Dongtie.

Talks with Russian Advisor

Industrial and Commercial Credit Loans - Banking Sector Decides to Continue 121

Awaiting Approval from the Ministry of Finance to Shanghai, the Subcommittee Will Convene to Study

Xinxin News Agency reports that regarding the issue of organizing a five million industrial and commercial credit loan, the Qianye Gonghui (Money Trade Association) has indicated that it will expand lending to the best of its ability and not participate in the banking syndicate. The banking syndicate organization will change its policy. The Banking Association subcommittee meeting must wait for the Ministry of Finance's approval of the case before convening a meeting to decide everything. The details learned by the Xinxin News Agency reporter are as follows:

The Banking Sector Decides to Continue

The five million yuan industrial and commercial credit loan, according to the original opinions of all parties, would be undertaken by the government for 2.5 million, the banking sector for 1.25 million, and the Qianye sector for 1.25 million. The three parties would jointly form a banking syndicate to handle the loan matters. Now that the Qianye sector has indicated that it will not participate in the banking syndicate, all sectors are paying close attention to whether the syndicate organization will change its policy. According to news from the banking sector, it is believed that the syndicate organization originally intended to proceed jointly by the three parties. Now that one party is unwilling to participate, the other two parties can still continue. This measure is for relief and also a duty that the financial sector should fulfill.

The Subcommittee Postpones the Meeting

The subcommittee organized by the Banking Association is entirely for the study of industrial and commercial credit loans. Regarding its meeting date, according to Lin Kanghou, the Secretary-General of the Banking Association, the subcommittee originally intended to convene a meeting to study the matter immediately. Now, because the Qianye sector has indicated that it will not participate and the banking syndicate organization should be changed, it must wait for the Ministry of Finance's approval of the case to Shanghai before scheduling a meeting to study the progress.

Yesterday, the association received a reply from the Municipal Council stating: "In reply to your letter of February 12th regarding the revision of water and electricity rates, the water rates were last implemented on April 1st of last year with an 80% discount for a period of one year. Now that the time limit has expired, the matter is under review. The increase in electricity prices is not purely due to the increase in coal prices, but is related to the increase in labor, warehouse goods, and other prices. Since the last revision of prices, prices have generally increased, and coal prices should only be considered as one of the elements. According to the items listed in the contract with the power company, if the circumstances for reducing prices are realized, the price will be reduced accordingly. This is a special reply."

Polish School Ship Arrives in Nagasaki for Repairs 124

Set to Sail to Shanghai Soon - Polish Goods Exhibition Ship Coming to the Far East

The Dar Pomorza, a school ship belonging to the Polish government's naval academy, carrying 66 students studying navigation and maritime commerce, and 41 crew members and professors, departed from Gdynia last September on a round-the-world voyage. It is now learned that the ship arrived in Yokohama, Japan, at the end of last month, and is currently docked in Nagasaki for repairs. It is expected to sail to Shanghai soon. Since it relies entirely on wind power, the exact date of arrival in Shanghai cannot be predicted. If there are no special winds or obstacles at sea, it may arrive by the end of this month, otherwise it may have to wait until the beginning of next month. The Polish community in Shanghai is preparing a grand welcome, and the Chinese government has designated the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Wusong Merchant Marine School to be responsible for the reception. In addition, Poland's total import volume for foreign trade last year was 79.7 million Polish zlotys, and its export volume was 97.5 million Polish zlotys, resulting in a surplus of 17.8 million Polish zlotys, an increase of 4.6 million Polish zlotys compared to the surplus of 13.3 million Polish zlotys in 1933. Overseas trade, such as with China, the United Kingdom, and Japan, has made considerable progress. Therefore, in order to develop overseas commerce, there are plans to establish consulates in important commercial ports such as China, Japan, and India. At the same time, two Polish goods exhibition ships will be sent to the United States and the Far East. The one sailing to the United States is the "Irmgard" and the one sailing to the East is the "Dadaros." The "Dadaros" exhibition ship is fully loaded with 10,000 tons of Polish goods. It departed from Gdynia, Poland, at the end of January and, after passing through Port Said, Penang, Suez, Singapore, and Hong Kong, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on April 20th. It is planned to invite people from all walks of life in Shanghai to board the ship for a public viewing on the 23rd, 24th, and 25th. Then, it will go to Dalian, and then to Kobe and Yokohama. Finally, the ship will return to Shanghai, and all the goods on board will be permanently displayed in the Polish General Chamber of Commerce in China.

The Ministry of Industry's Fishery Protection Office Protects Fishermen 129

Proclamation to Severely Punish Traitors Who Borrow Names and Parade Around

The Ministry of Industry believes that the peak season for fishing is imminent. In order to protect fishermen, in addition to consulting the Ministry of the Navy and the coastal provincial governments to assist in protecting fisheries, it has also ordered the Fishery Protection Office to instruct the patrol ships to prepare to depart and protect fishing boats. Yuan Lianghua, the Director of the Fishery Protection Office, issued the following proclamation to prevent unscrupulous people from borrowing names and parading around: "For the matter of proclamation, it is the responsibility of this office to protect fisheries. Each fishing season, patrol ships are dispatched to patrol the waters of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to protect fishing and never receive protection fees or any subsidies. This has been proclaimed in the past. Fearing that it may be ignored over time, this proclamation is issued again. If there are any treacherous people who impersonate this office, parade around outside, and collect any fees, they will be severely investigated and punished. All fishermen must be informed. If any of the above circumstances are discovered, they should be immediately brought to this office or patrol ships for investigation, or reported to this office for punishment. This is a proclamation."

The Silk Industry Bank Promotes Commercial Acceptance Drafts 131

A Letter to the Banking Association Requesting Consistent Implementation - Also a Letter to the Silk and Satin Industry Association

Since the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association created commercial acceptance drafts with the aim of reducing the account period and increasing currency utilization, the public has paid close attention to this issue. After receiving the association's letter requesting discounts upon implementation, the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank convened a meeting of important officials and decided to first promote and provide discounts as much as possible in accordance with regulations, and is planning convenient and simple discount procedures for these drafts. At the same time, it is believed that once these drafts are circulated, because they are indeed in line with the current needs of industry and commerce, it is expected that various industries will follow the silk and satin industry and imitate them. The relationship with the business of various banks in Shanghai will also become increasingly practical. Therefore, the bank suggested that the Shanghai Banking Association discuss this matter when it convenes a meeting in order to gather ideas and benefit the public, so that these notes can be easily promoted and the discount system can be perfected. It is heard that the Banking Association, according to the Silk Industry Bank's letter, established a subcommittee yesterday and appointed nine banks, including China, Communications, Shanghai, Guohua, Silk, and Xinhua, to formulate detailed implementation measures. It is expected that the circulation of these commercial notes will become more widespread day by day. The original letters from the Silk Industry Bank to the Banking Association and the reply to the Silk and Satin Industry Association are copied below:

Letter to the Banking Association

"Dear Sirs, we have received your letter of March 8th stating that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's letter regarding the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association's creation of commercial acceptance drafts was forwarded to the banks in the association for review. We have also received a separate letter from the association stating that the association has resolved to create commercial acceptance drafts at a temporary members' meeting, with the aim of reducing the account period and increasing currency utilization. The benefits of its application are that the seller has a definite period for short-term collection of the goods, and can also hold it to banks and money shops for discounting. The buyer pays on schedule without any preparation. For banks and money shops, this acceptance draft is jointly responsible by the issuer and the acceptor, and the term is not long. If discounting is accepted, it is more secure and reliable than credit lending. It has a safe way to grow profits and can support the development of industry and commerce. Your association is known to be an up-and-coming force in the banking sector, paying attention to financial regulation and social services, and our silk and satin industry benefits even more because of business relationships. Therefore, the establishment has grown rapidly in just a few years, and its reputation is growing. It is also timely to take the lead and create new achievements, and industry and commerce are benefiting greatly. The commercial acceptance draft created by our colleagues is in line with your association's usual purpose and is expected to be supported. We hope that you will take the lead in allowing discounts when implemented to benefit industry and commerce. Commercial bills have been in use in various countries for a long time, so the discounting business has developed accordingly, and the discounting market should be established in response. Now that the association has created the aforementioned drafts, it is indeed in line with the current needs of industry and commerce. It is expected that various industries will follow suit, and its function to indirectly promote banking business is worth supporting. Our bank is approving the methods for accepting discounts. Once it is settled, we will send a special letter to inform the association. However, political matters are important, and we hope that your association will raise it for discussion when convening a meeting, so that we can gather ideas and benefit the public, and the implementation will be more helpful. It is expected that this discounting system will become more perfect, and fellow industries can also benefit a lot in business."

Reply to the Silk Industry Association

"Dear Sirs, we have received your letter stating that your association has resolved to create commercial acceptance drafts in accordance with the bill law at a temporary members' meeting, with the aim of reducing the account period and increasing currency utilization, which is the same as our bank's usual purpose of serving society. We intend to negotiate discounts when implemented in order to facilitate circulation. At this time of industrial and commercial depression, the circulation of this bill is a unique and effective policy for increasing leverage, regulating finance, and restoring all industries. We are in awe of your association's leaders who initiated the compass for merchants to prescribe the right medicine. The bank originally aimed to regulate surpluses and deficits, and circulation is its responsibility. For this commercial acceptance draft, it should be supported and promoted. If your colleagues implement it on schedule, our bank will accept discounts as much as possible in line with its usual purpose of service to facilitate elegant life. As for the discount procedures, our bank is planning convenient and simple methods in order to make promotion easier. Moreover, commercial bills have been in use in various countries for a long time, and the discounting business has also developed accordingly. The discounting market has emerged in response. Now, the drafts created by your association are in line with the world trend and the current needs of industry and commerce. It is expected that various industries will follow suit, which requires the cooperation of the entire financial industry to achieve its full success and achieve its great effect. Therefore, in addition to accepting your association's commission to discount this bill as much as possible in accordance with regulations, we have already asked the Shanghai Banking Association to raise it for discussion when convening a meeting to formulate a detailed plan, so that this bill will be more easily promoted, the discount system will become more perfect, and the national economy will benefit from it. Is it only one industry that benefits from it? This is a special reply, and I hope you will consider it."

Chamber of Commerce Informs the Public Security Bureau Regarding Lost Pawn Tickets and Affixing Stamps: Old Books Need Not Be Restamped Unless Continued in Use 137

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau explaining the responsibility for affixing stamps to lost pawn tickets. The letter states that lost pawn tickets and pawn receipts are documents issued by pawnshops to pawners to protect their rights. According to the provisional regulations on stamp tax, the responsibility for affixing stamps lies with the pawner who issued the document. For example, if a shop fails to affix a stamp to an invoice, the person who issued and received the invoice will be fined. The pawnshop should not be held responsible for the pawner's fault. Regarding account book stamps, according to the regulations, a stamp worth one dime should be affixed to each book each year. If a new book is used in the following year and the old book is not continued, then there is no need to affix additional stamps to the old book. This is the natural interpretation of the regulations and has been the practice for many years. Whether the old book from the previous year is continued in use depends on whether new accounts are added to it. Each pawnshop's book is a volume per month and has a starting and ending point. The serial numbers have long been assigned. Therefore, the new accounts in the following year will not be connected to the old book from the previous year. All of this is clear to anyone who understands accounting and business practices. Placing old accounts on the desk or in the account box is for the same purpose: for reference. There is no law requiring additional stamps to be affixed to old accounts when they are inspected. The public association's statement is alarming. Except for one account book with a missing stamp, which should be sent to the court for punishment by your bureau according to regulations, the remaining six account books with sufficient stamps, as well as the nine pawn tickets and one pawn receipt, should be returned to us to maintain fairness and to inform the inspectors to handle the matter carefully in the future. This is our earnest request.

Shanghai Industrial Trust Society to Take Over Gaoqiao Seaside Bathing Beach and Expand It According to Plan 140

The Gaoqiao Seaside Bathing Beach is a natural sandy beach, vast and boundless, with flat terrain and water levels of varying depths, making it a natural place for sea bathing and swimming. Since the Seaside Hotel leased and operated it, many people have gone there every summer. However, the hotel is limited by its finances, and it is difficult to achieve perfect facilities. Therefore, the Shanghai Industrial Trust Society will take it over this year and run it municipally. Inquiring about various situations, they are recorded below:

Preparing Funds to Take Over

The Gaoqiao Seaside Hotel has been leased and operated for several years. Although there were few visitors at first, the investment in facilities has exceeded tens of thousands. Although the business has recently developed gradually, the shareholders do not intend to continue operating it because the expansion of facilities is beyond their ability. Therefore, the Shanghai Industrial Trust Society has prepared funds to take it over. The two parties have reached an agreement through negotiations, and the society will expand it.

Planning Expansion

According to news obtained from the society, the society will focus on the following points when expanding and reorganizing the seaside bathing beach: (1) Reorganize the sandy beach, flatten the fine sand, and sift out the stones; (2) Build a large-scale cafeteria, selling Chinese food, snacks, cold drinks, etc.; (3) Build rain showers, changing rooms, and rent out high-quality bathing suits; (4) Plant flowers and trees extensively and set up wisteria trellises; (5) Provide遊boats and small boats for tourists to use. The above projects are estimated to cost 50,000 to 60,000.

Shen Bao Circulation Library Increases Reading Room Hours 142

Open from 9:30 AM Every Day; Open as Usual on Mondays to Read Newspapers

The purpose of the Shen Bao Circulation Library was originally to be a circulation library. Later, at the request of the guardians, a reading room was opened next to the lending desk to read books, magazines, and newspapers. The library currently displays more than 180 kinds of relatively advanced magazines, more than 40 kinds of newspapers, and various magazine compilations. You can take them out and read them at will. The average number of readers per day has reached more than 450 people. It is open every morning and closes at 6:00 PM in the afternoon. It is closed one day on Monday. Recently, some readers proposed on the library's bulletin board that it should be open from 9:00 AM in the morning and that it should not be closed on Mondays. Now, in order to respect the readers' opinions, the library's board of directors has decided that it will be open from 9:30 AM every morning, and the closing time in the afternoon will remain the same. It will be open on Mondays during the regular hours so that readers will not be interrupted from reading newspapers every day. However, due to time constraints, there are fewer books and magazines. It will still not be lent out or read on Mondays. This decision will be implemented starting this Monday.

The Second Landlord of the House Is Japanese; Whether Everyone Is Arrested Is Unknown

Lu Liankui, the Chinese Superintendent of the General Inspectorate, and Song Bingzheng, the detective, learned that there was a large-scale drug manufacturing facility for heroin on the upper floor of a four-story Western-style building at 45, Lane 512, Bazilu. They issued Search Warrant No. 6134 to the First Special District Court and went secretly with West Detective Pullat at 11:30 AM the day before yesterday. It was found that the second landlord of the house was a Japanese named Yi Yaxi who rented it. The Japanese Police Department was notified to send a Japanese detective to enter the house together. It was learned that the drug manufacturing facility was on the fourth floor. Without making a sound, they calmly went up. It was already after 2:00 PM. The workers in the room were about to start working when they heard the news and fled in a hurry. Four local people, Ma Rongmei, Zhang Xiaodi, Hu Afa from Shaoxing, and Li Abao from Yangzhou, were arrested outside the door. Two barrels of heroin weighing 37 pounds, two large cans of raw materials weighing 19 pounds, and a package of crude materials weighing 3 pounds were seized and taken to the Hongkou Police Station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Public Works Bureau detailed the previous situation and said that the house was said to have been sublet to a Chinese named Wang Dingru by the Japanese Yi. The defendants denied being workers in the facility at the police station, but when they were arrested, their hands were white. He requested that they be detained for further investigation. Although the large number of machines and objects in the manufacturing room were now guarded by Chinese and Japanese detectives and were not allowed to be moved, it would be best to ask the court to conduct an on-site inspection. When questioned, the defendants hesitated and denied working in the heroin manufacturing facility on the fourth floor.
